SESSION: 2026-03-04 - Feature #260
==================================================

## What was accomplished:

### Feature #260: Keyboard Bulk Node Movement (PASSING)
- Added moveNodes batch method to coreStore.ts:
  - Takes array of {nodeId, x, y} moves and optional snapshot description
  - Applies all moves to graph in sequence using engineMoveNode
  - Clamps coordinates to Math.max(0, value) to prevent negative positions
  - Takes single undo snapshot after all moves complete
  - Updates isDirty, canUndo, canRedo state
- Added Alt+Arrow keyboard handler in Canvas.tsx:
  - Alt+Arrow: moves selected nodes by 20px (SMALL_STEP)
  - Shift+Alt+Arrow: moves selected nodes by 100px (LARGE_STEP)
  - Uses capture phase event listener
  - Skips when text input focused, dialogs open, Connect mode, placement mode
  - Builds batch moves from current graph positions of selected nodes
  - Calls moveNodes with formatted description "Move N node(s)"
- Added CSS transition in index.css:
  - .react-flow__node { transition: transform 150ms ease-out }
  - .react-flow__node.dragging { transition: none } (disables during drag)

## Test file: test/unit/ui/keyboardBulkNodeMovement.test.ts (49 tests, all passing)

15-19. Negative coordinate clamping: x clamped, y clamped, both clamped, positive not affected, partial clamping
20. Non-selected nodes not affected
21-28. Step sizes: 20px/100px constants, all 4 directions with both step sizes
29-31. Properties preserved: type, displayName, width/height
32-35. Edge cases: empty moves, duplicate node in batch, non-existent ID, zero position
36-37. CSS transition: transition rule exists, dragging disables it
38-46. Source code verification: handler exists, shiftKey check, moveNodes method, clamping, single snapshot, preventDefault, Connect mode skip, text input skip, store subscription
47-49. Integration workflows: select 3 → Alt+Right → undo → restored, Shift+Alt+Down → undo, sequential moves with separate undo snapshots

  blocking the action in Normal mode
- 25 unit tests in test/unit/ui/quickRenameF2.test.ts

### Feature #244: Command Palette Node Creation (PASSING)
- Discovered getNodeCreationCommands() was already fully implemented in commandRegistry.ts
- Wrote 29 comprehensive tests verifying: command generation, search keywords, execute,
  nested navigation, getAllCommands integration
- Fixed nested navigation test: needed to create actual parent node first
- Test file: test/unit/ui/commandPaletteNodeCreation.test.ts

### Feature #246: Keyboard Node Deletion with Undo Hint (PASSING)
- Created toast notification system:
  - Added toastMessage/toastTimerId state + showToast/clearToast actions to uiStore
  - Created src/components/shared/Toast.tsx component (fixed bottom-center, auto-dismiss 4s)
  - Added <Toast /> to App.tsx
- Enhanced DeleteConfirmationDialog:
  - Added Enter key confirmation (keyboard accessible)
  - Added toast after deletion: "Deleted {name}. Cmd+Z to undo"
- Added edge deletion via Delete key in Canvas.tsx (direct, no confirmation)
- Fixed critical mode filter bug in useKeyboardShortcuts.ts:
  - Old: `if (actionId.startsWith('edit:') && currentMode !== CanvasMode.Edit) return;`
  - New: `if (actionId === 'edit:exit' && currentMode !== CanvasMode.Edit) return;`
  - This was blocking edit:undo, edit:redo, edit:delete in Normal mode
- 18 unit tests in test/unit/ui/keyboardDeletionWithUndo.test.ts
- Browser verified: node delete+toast+undo, edge delete+toast all working

## Key bug fixes:
- Mode filter was overly broad, blocking ALL edit:* actions in Normal mode.
  Only edit:exit (the mode transition action) should be gated by mode.
  Category-based actions (edit:undo, edit:redo, edit:delete) work in ALL modes.

### Feature #238: Autosave on Focus Change (PASSING)
- Created useAutoSaveOnBlur hook (src/hooks/useAutoSaveOnBlur.ts):
  - Listens for both 'visibilitychange' (tab hidden) and 'blur' (window blur) events
  - Checks all conditions before saving: autosaveOnBlur enabled, isDirty, !isSaving, fileHandle exists
  - fileHandle required (can't show file picker when tab is hidden)

  - Shows "Autosaved" status message in green in status bar for 3 seconds
  - Cleans up event listeners and timeouts on unmount
- Added autosave preference state to uiStore.ts:

SESSION: 2026-03-03 - Feature #227
==================================================

## What was accomplished:

### Feature #227: File header timestamps set correctly on save (PASSING)
- Verified complete implementation already in place across the full save/load pipeline:
  - codec.ts encode(): Sets createdAtMs to Date.now() on first save (when missing/0), always updates updatedAtMs
  - fileIO.ts graphToProto(): Passes createdAtMs through to header if provided
  - fileIO.ts protoToGraphFull(): Extracts createdAtMs and updatedAtMs from decoded file header
  - coreStore.ts: Tracks fileCreatedAtMs in state, passes to save functions to preserve across re-saves
- 15 comprehensive unit tests already exist and all pass:
  1. First save sets createdAtMs to current time
  2. Every save updates updatedAtMs
  3. Preserves createdAtMs on re-save when passed explicitly
  4. Does NOT change createdAtMs on re-save
  5. updatedAtMs changes on each re-save
  6. protoToGraphFull extracts both timestamps from header

## What was accomplished:

### Feature #214: Double-click Add Note doesn't create duplicate notes (PASSING)
- Added useRef-based savingNoteRef guard in NotesTab component (NodeDetailPanel.tsx)
- The guard prevents handleSave from executing twice on rapid double-click:
  - First Save: sets savingNoteRef.current = true, calls onAddNote, closes editor
  - Second Save: savingNoteRef.current is true → returns immediately (no duplicate)
- Guard lifecycle:
  - Resets to false on handleOpenEditor (new editor session)
  - Resets to false on handleCancel (so next note creation works)
  - Stays true after save until editor opens again (prevents race condition)
- Also added useRef import to the file's React import line

## Test file: test/unit/ui/doubleClickAddNote.test.ts (27 tests, all passing)

   - After Save + new editor, three sequential notes, cancel + new note

SESSION: 2026-03-03 - Feature #212
==================================================

## What was accomplished:

### Feature #212: Double-click save doesn't corrupt file (PASSING)
- Added `isSaving` boolean guard flag to coreStore state
- Guard prevents concurrent saves from double-click or rapid Ctrl+S:
  - saveFile() checks `if (get().isSaving) return false` at entry
  - saveFileAs() checks the same guard at entry
  - Both methods set `isSaving: true` before starting, reset to `false` on success/error/cancel
  - Cross-method protection: saveFile blocks saveFileAs and vice versa
- Console logs "[CoreStore] Save already in progress, ignoring duplicate request" when rejecting duplicate save

## Test file: test/unit/store/doubleClickSave.test.ts (19 tests, all passing)
1. isSaving starts as false
2. isSaving becomes true while save is in progress
3. Second saveFile() call returns false while first is in progress
4. saveArchcFile is called only once when save is triggered twice rapidly
5. isSaving resets to false after successful save
6. isSaving resets to false after failed save
7. Can save again after first save completes
8. Can save again after first save fails
9. Second saveFileAs() call returns false while first is in progress
10. saveArchcFileAs is called only once for rapid double-click
11. isSaving resets to false after saveFileAs user cancels
12. isSaving resets to false after saveFileAs error
13. saveFileAs blocked while saveFile is in progress
14. saveFile blocked while saveFileAs is in progress
15. isDirty is correctly cleared after single save succeeds
16. isDirty remains true when second save is rejected
17. Graph state remains consistent after rapid save attempts
18. Three rapid saves only execute one save operation
19. Console logs message when duplicate save is rejected

## Browser verification steps completed:
1. Loaded ecommerce.archc: 5 nodes, 4 edges, ✓ Saved ✓
2. Created new file (Ctrl+N) ✓
3. Added Service node → Nodes: 1, ● Modified ✓
4. Pressed Ctrl+S twice rapidly → no crashes, no errors ✓
5. Console: 0 errors, 0 warnings ✓
6. Reloaded ecommerce.archc → all 5 nodes, 4 edges intact ✓
7. Mock data grep: only legitimate globalThis.crypto in codec.ts ✓

## Implementation approach:
- Store-level `isSaving` flag is the simplest and most reliable approach
- Checked at the very start of saveFile() and saveFileAs() (before any async work)
- Uses synchronous Zustand state updates for immediate lock acquisition
- Properly cleared in all code paths (try/catch/finally equivalent)
- No debouncing needed — just a boolean guard that blocks concurrent saves

SESSION: 2026-03-02 - Features #145, #146, #147
==================================================

## What was accomplished:

### Feature #145: Node deletion via Delete/Backspace key (PASSING)
- Added Delete and Backspace key handlers to Canvas component
- Delete key always triggers deletion dialog when a node is selected
- Backspace triggers deletion at root level (zooms out when in navigation path)
- Disabled React Flow's built-in deleteKeyCode to prevent conflicts
- Used capture-phase event listener for reliable key interception
- Ignores keystrokes in input/textarea fields
- Prevents double-trigger when dialog is already open

### Feature #146: Deletion confirmation dialog shows cascade impact (PASSING)
- Created DeleteConfirmationDialog component in src/components/shared/
- Shows node name being deleted (bold)
- Yellow alert box showing cascade impact: N connected edges, N child nodes
- Cancel and Confirm (Delete) buttons with clear visual hierarchy
- Escape key closes dialog, backdrop click closes dialog
- "This action can be undone with Ctrl+Z" message
- Alert triangle warning icon
- z-100 overlay with semi-transparent backdrop

### Feature #147: Node deletion removes connected edges (PASSING)
- Graph engine's removeNode() already handled cascading edge removal
- Created deletionImpact utility (src/core/graph/deletionImpact.ts) for calculating impact
- Verified: Deleting API Gateway (2 edges) → 5→4 nodes, 4→2 edges
- Verified: Deleting Order Service (2 edges) → 5→4 nodes, 4→2 edges
- Other connected nodes preserved correctly

## Technical details:
- Key insight: React Flow v12 has deleteKeyCode='Backspace' by default, which intercepts
  Backspace before custom handlers. Fixed with deleteKeyCode={null} on ReactFlow component.
- Capture-phase event listener (addEventListener('keydown', handler, true)) ensures our
  handler runs before React Flow's internal event handling.
- uiStore extended with deleteDialogOpen/deleteDialogInfo state management.
- DeleteConfirmationDialog uses Zustand stores: useUIStore for dialog state, useCoreStore
  for removeNode action, useCanvasStore for clearing selection after deletion.

## Current completion status:
- Features passing: 67+ of 235 (~28.5%)
- Zero console errors
- All implementations verified via browser automation on Playwright

- Edge deletion features (Delete key on selected edge)

  - readFormatVersion() utility to inspect version without full decode

  7. Rejects 65535 (max uint16)
  8. Rejects 256
  9. Does NOT reject current FORMAT_VERSION
  10. Does NOT reject version 0
  11. readFormatVersion reads future version correctly
  12. readFormatVersion reads current version correctly
  13. Thrown error is CodecError instance
  14. Version check before checksum verification

   - Wire type 6 on unknown field → CodecError

   - String field length exceeds buffer → CodecError

   - FileHeader format_version as string → CodecError
   - Architecture name as varint → CodecError

   - Corrupted nested Node position → error or safe decode
   - Edge with impossibly large enum value → handled safely

   - Non-integer format_version → "header.formatVersion: integer expected"

   - Non-string Node.id → "id: string expected"
   - Non-number Position.x → "number expected"
   - Valid message → null (no error)

   - Valid file passes both decode and verify
   - Protobuf decode errors wrapped as CodecError
7. All malformation errors are proper Error instances (4 tests)
   - Invalid wire type → Error subclass
   - Excessive length → Error subclass
   - Deeply nested corruption → Error subclass, no crash
   - Multiple sequential variants → all proper errors
8. Error messages identify the malformed area (3 tests)
   - verify error includes field path (e.g., "header.formatVersion")
   - Nested node field includes full path
   - Codec decode error includes protobuf context
9. User-visible error dialog integration (2 tests)
   - Malformed data maps to "Invalid File Format" dialog
   - Error dialog dismissible, app continues

    - Valid file passes both decode and verify
    - Empty architecture passes verify

SESSION: 2026-03-03 - Feature #250
==================================================

## What was accomplished:

### Feature #250: Vim-style Connect Mode (PASSING)
- Implemented full Vim-style edge creation workflow:
  1. Press C with node selected → enters Connect mode, source = selected node
  2. Press C without selection → enters Connect mode, must pick source first
  3. Arrow keys in Connect mode → spatial navigation to pick target node
  4. Enter → confirms target → shows type picker
  5. 1/2/3 keys → picks edge type (1=Sync, 2=Async, 3=Data Flow)
  6. Edge created, undo snapshot taken, returns to Normal mode, new edge selected
  7. Escape at any step → cancels, clears state, returns to Normal

- Added to uiStore:
  - connectSource, connectTarget, connectStep state
  - startConnect(), setConnectTarget(), setConnectStep(), clearConnectState() actions
  - exitToNormal() now also clears connect state

- Modified Canvas.tsx:
  - Connect mode keyboard handler (arrow keys, Enter, 1/2/3) in capture phase
  - Normal arrow handler skips when in Connect mode
  - Preview dashed edge (animated, blue, strokeDasharray) from source to target
  - Source node green glow CSS class (connect-source-glow)
  - Connect mode overlay banner showing step-specific instructions

- Modified useKeyboardShortcuts.ts:
  - C key now calls startConnect(selectedNodeId) when entering Connect mode

- Added to index.css:
  - .react-flow__node.connect-source-glow: green box-shadow + border-radius

SESSION: 2026-03-04 - Feature #267
==================================================

## What was accomplished:

### Feature #267: Idempotent dev server launcher script (PASSING)

Created scripts/ensure-dev-server.sh - an idempotent launcher that ensures exactly
one Vite dev server is running on port 5173:

**Script features:**
- Health check: curl to localhost:5173, exits 0 immediately if server already running
- Atomic lock: mkdir-based lock prevents concurrent launches (race-condition safe)
- Double-check after lock: re-checks port after acquiring lock
- Background startup: nohup npm run dev, polls until ready (max 30s, 0.5s intervals)
- Process monitoring: detects if server process dies during startup
- PID file tracking: stores PID for reliable stop
- --stop flag: kills running server via PID file or lsof fallback
- Cleanup: lock auto-removed via trap EXIT

**Configuration changes:**
1. vite.config.ts: Added `strictPort: true` - Vite now errors if port 5173 is taken
   instead of silently using 5174+
2. package.json: Added `dev:ensure` and `dev:stop` npm scripts
3. playwright.config.ts: webServer.command changed from `npm run dev` to `npm run dev:ensure`

**Testing completed:**
- First run: starts server successfully (exit 0)
- Idempotency: 5 sequential runs all exit 0 without spawning new processes
- Stop/restart: `dev:stop` kills server, `dev:ensure` restarts it
- strictPort: Second Vite on port 5173 fails with "Port 5173 is already in use"
- Lock bypass: Script detects running server before checking lock (fast path)
- Browser verification: App loads correctly at localhost:5173
- Console: 0 errors, 0 warnings
- All 3242 existing tests pass (155 test files)
- No mock data patterns in production code

- Fully implemented NativeFileSystemAdapter:

  - saveFile(): Filesystem.writeFile() to existing path or default Documents/ArchCanvas/
  - saveFileAs(): Filesystem.writeFile() to Documents + Share.share() for iOS export

#### Implementation:

  - Narrow viewport (1024px) → floor 180px

- test/unit/cli/queryCommands.test.ts: 37 tests

#### Issues found and fixed:
1. **Diagnostic log pollution**: console.log from [TextApi], [RegistryManager], [ExportApi]
   constructors was going to stdout, breaking JSON pipe output.
   - Added suppressDiagnosticLogs() in src/cli/index.ts that redirects [bracketed] logs to stderr
   - Applied in loadContext() and list-nodedefs command
   - Applied same fix in src/cli/commands/query.ts

2. **Protobuf ESM import**: src/proto/archcanvas.pb.js used `import * as $protobuf from "protobufjs/minimal"`
   which doesn't work in Node.js ESM (tsx). Changed to `import $protobufDefault from "protobufjs/minimal"`
   with CJS→ESM normalization.

3. **Test fixture bug**: queryCommands.test.ts used `targetNodeId` instead of `nodeId` in addNote params.

- All 37 query command tests passing

## Session: Feature #307 - CLI Output Formatting (JSON, Table, Human-Readable)
Date: 2026-03-04

### Feature #307: CLI Output Formatting - PASSING

#### Implementation:
Created a shared output formatting module used by all CLI commands.

- src/cli/formatter.ts (new file):
  - formatAsJson(data): JSON.stringify with 2-space indent
  - formatAsTable(headers, rows): ASCII table with column alignment, minWidth, right-align support
  - formatAsHuman(template, data): template-based human-readable output with {key} placeholders
  - formatNodeSummary(): formats node lists in json/table/human modes
  - formatNodeDetail(): formats single node detail in all modes
  - formatEdgeSummary(): formats edge lists with arrow notation in human mode
  - formatSearchResult(): formats search results with type badges and scores
  - formatOutput(): generic format dispatcher for any data
  - writeOutput(): sends data to stdout (console.log)
  - writeInfo(): sends info messages to stderr (console.error), respects --quiet
  - writeError(): sends error messages to stderr with "Error:" prefix

- src/cli/index.ts:
  - Replaced inline printOutput implementation with formatter module delegation
  - Re-exports all formatter functions for backward compatibility
  - printOutput now calls formatOutput + writeOutput

- src/cli/commands/mutate.ts:
  - Replaced console.log info messages with writeInfo (goes to stderr)
  - Replaced printOutput calls with formatAsJson + writeOutput
  - All 6 mutation commands updated

## Session: Feature #340 - Filesystem Scanner with Gitignore Support
Date: 2026-03-04

### Feature #340: Filesystem Scanner with Gitignore Support - PASSING

#### Implementation:
Created src/analyze/scanner.ts with a complete filesystem scanning module:

- **parseGitignore(content)**: Parses .gitignore file content into structured rules
  - Handles comments, empty lines, negation (!), directory-only patterns (trailing /)
  - Converts gitignore glob patterns to RegExp (supports *, **, ?, [])
  - Handles escaped characters and path-relative vs basename matching

- **isIgnored(relativePath, isDirectory, rules)**: Tests if a path matches ignore rules
  - Processes rules in order, last match wins (supports negation override)
  - Respects directory-only patterns

- **scanDirectory(rootPath, options)**: Main entry point
  - Recursive directory walking using Node.js fs APIs
  - Merges .gitignore rules at each directory level
  - Built-in ignores: node_modules, .git, dist, build, __pycache__, target, vendor, etc.
  - Configurable: maxDepth (default 10), maxFiles (default 10000), additionalIgnore patterns
  - Returns ScanResult: { fileTree, totalFiles, totalDirs, languageBreakdown }
  - FileTree has nested DirectoryEntry/FileEntry structure
  - Each FileEntry has: name, relativePath, size, extension, lastModified
  - Sorted entries for deterministic output

#### Tests (test/unit/analyze/scanner.test.ts):
- 26 tests all passing
- parseGitignore: simple patterns, comments, negation, escaped chars
- isIgnored: filenames, directory-only, negation, path separators, **, ?
- scanDirectory: simple files, nested dirs, metadata, built-in ignores, .gitignore respect,
  nested .gitignore, maxDepth, maxFiles, additionalIgnore, language breakdown,
  relative paths, empty dirs, sorting, defaults, non-existent dir

#### Committed: 9275b77
#### Features passing: 332+ of 340+

### Feature #341: Project Type and Framework Detector - PASSING

#### Implementation:
Created src/analyze/detector.ts with comprehensive project analysis capabilities:

- **detectLanguages(scanResult)**: Detects languages from file extension distribution and config files (package.json→JS/TS, go.mod→Go, Cargo.toml→Rust, requirements.txt→Python, pom.xml→Java, etc.)
- **detectFrameworks(scanResult)**: Detects frameworks from config files (Next.js, Vite, Angular, Django, Spring Boot, etc.) and file extensions (.tsx→React, .vue→Vue, .svelte→Svelte)
- **detectProjectType(scanResult)**: Classifies as monorepo (lerna/turbo/nx/workspaces), microservices (multiple Dockerfiles), library, or single-app
- **detectBuildSystems(scanResult)**: Identifies npm, yarn, pnpm, cargo, go modules, maven, gradle, make, etc.
- **detectInfraSignals(scanResult)**: Detects Docker, Kubernetes, Terraform, CI/CD (GitHub Actions, GitLab, Jenkins, CircleCI, Travis), cloud platforms
- **detectDataStores(scanResult)**: Finds Prisma, Drizzle, SQLite, TypeORM, Knex, Firebase, Protocol Buffers
- **detectEntryPoints(scanResult)**: Identifies common entry points (src/index.ts, main.go, manage.py, etc.)
- **detectProject(scanResult)**: Main API returning complete ProjectProfile

#### Types exported:
- ProjectProfile, DetectedLanguage, DetectedFramework, ProjectType, InfraSignal, DetectedDataStore

## Session: Feature #342 - Key File Selector and Content Extractor
Date: 2026-03-04

### Feature #342: Key File Selector and Content Extractor - PASSING

#### Implementation:
Created src/analyze/fileSelector.ts with intelligent file selection and content extraction:

- **selectKeyFiles(scanResult, projectProfile, options)**: Main API function
  - 4-tier priority system for file selection:
    - Tier 1 (always include): package.json, go.mod, Cargo.toml, Dockerfile, docker-compose.yml, README.md, tsconfig.json, etc.
    - Tier 2 (high value): entry points (src/index.ts, main.go, etc.), route definitions (routes.ts, urls.py), schema files (.proto, .graphql, openapi.yaml, schema.prisma)
    - Tier 3 (structural): module index files (index.ts, __init__.py, mod.rs)
    - Tier 4 (representative): 1-2 sample source files per major directory
  - Smart content truncation: reads up to maxLinesPerFile (default 500), adds truncation notice
  - Token budget: caps total extracted content at totalTokenBudget (default 100K tokens)
  - Deduplication: files classified in multiple tiers are only included once at highest priority
  - Configurable via FileSelectionOptions: maxLinesPerFile, totalTokenBudget, rootDir, skipContentRead

- **Types exported**: FileTier, SelectedFile, KeyFileSet, FileSelectionOptions

#### Tests (test/unit/analyze/fileSelector.test.ts):
- 44 tests all passing
- Tier 1: package.json, go.mod, Cargo.toml, Dockerfile, docker-compose.yml, README.md, tsconfig.json, multiple Tier 1 files
- Tier 2: entry points (src/index.ts, main.go, main.py), detected entry points from profile, route definitions (routes.ts, router.js, urls.py), schema files (.proto, .graphql, openapi.yaml, schema.prisma)
- Tier 3: index.ts barrels, __init__.py, mod.rs, index.js
- Tier 4: representative files, 2-per-dir limit, no duplication with higher tiers, source-only filtering
- Token budget: respects limit, default 100K, provides totalTokenEstimate
- Tier ordering: 1 before 2, 2 before 3, priority on tight budget
- Return format: KeyFileSet structure, empty scan handling
- Multi-project types: Node.js/TS, Go, Python, Rust
- Deduplication and options tests

#### Verification:
- 142 total analyze tests passing (44 new + 72 detector + 26 scanner)
- Build succeeds cleanly
- No mock data patterns in production code

## Session: Feature #343 - AI Architecture Inference Engine
Date: 2026-03-04

### Feature #343: AI Architecture Inference Engine - PASSING

#### Implementation:
Created src/analyze/inferEngine.ts with comprehensive AI-powered architecture inference:

- **inferArchitecture(sender, projectProfile, keyFiles, options)**: Main API function
  - Takes an AIMessageSender (dependency injection for testability)
  - Takes ProjectProfile from detector.ts and KeyFileSet from fileSelector.ts
  - Returns InferenceResult with nodes, edges, architecture name/description

- **Analysis Depth Modes**:
  - 'quick': Single prompt, structure-only analysis (1 AI call)
  - 'standard': Multi-step analysis (3 AI calls): identify components → relationships → map to types
  - 'deep': Standard + refinement step (4 AI calls): adds detailed notes and suggestions

- **Zod Validation**: inferenceResultSchema validates AI responses with recursive node schema
  - InferredNode: id, type, displayName, description, codeRefs[], children[] (recursive)
  - InferredEdge: from, to, type (SYNC/ASYNC/DATA_FLOW), label
  - InferredCodeRef: path, role (SOURCE/API_SPEC/SCHEMA/DEPLOYMENT/CONFIG/TEST)
  - Step-specific schemas for intermediate validation

- **extractJson()**: Robust JSON extraction from AI text (handles markdown fences, surrounding text)
- **batchFiles()**: Splits files into batches that fit within token limits
- **mergeResults()**: Deduplicates and merges results from multiple inference batches
- **sendWithRetry()**: Exponential backoff retry logic (configurable maxRetries, 30s max delay)
- **Streaming**: onProgress callback for step-by-step progress, onChunk for text streaming
- **Abort support**: AbortSignal propagation through all async operations

- **AIMessageSender interface**: Dependency injection for the AI client
  - Allows testing without real API calls
  - Compatible with existing src/ai/client.ts sendMessage function

- **Built-in Node Types**: All 15 node types included in prompts:
  - Compute: service, function, worker, api-gateway
  - Data: database, cache, object-storage, repository
  - Messaging: message-queue, event-bus, stream-processor
  - Network: load-balancer, cdn
  - Observability: logging, monitoring

#### Tests (test/unit/analyze/inferEngine.test.ts): 49 tests
- extractJson: plain text, markdown fences, nested objects, surrounding text
- batchFiles: single batch, multi-batch, oversized files, empty input
- mergeResults: single result, dedup nodes/edges, architecture name from first
- inferenceResultSchema: valid data, missing fields, empty nodes, invalid edge types, recursive children, code ref roles
- inferArchitecture quick: valid result, single call, project profile in prompt, node types in prompt, file contents, markdown fences, progress events, streaming
- inferArchitecture standard: 3 AI calls, progress events per step, partial results
- inferArchitecture deep: 4 AI calls, step 4 refinement event
- Error handling: invalid JSON, schema validation, raw response in errors, retry logic, max retries exceeded, abort signal
- Token batching: multi-batch merge in quick mode
- Profile formatting: infra signals, data stores, empty profile

#### Verification:
- 191 total analyze tests passing (49 new + 142 existing)
- TypeScript compiles with no errors (tsc --noEmit)
- No mock data patterns in production code
- Committed: c2a6bdc

#### Current completion status:
- Feature #343 marked passing
- Features passing: 343 of 349 (98.3%)

## Session: Feature #366 - Node text remains readable across all color tints and themes
Date: 2026-03-05

### Feature #366: Node text readable across all color tints and themes - PASSING

#### Analysis:
Performed comprehensive text contrast analysis across all 12 accent colors (Blue, Green, Orange, Purple, Cyan, Red, Pink, Indigo, Teal, Amber, Lime, Rose) in both dark and light modes.

Key findings:
1. All icon badge contrast ratios >= 3.0:1 (WCAG AA for large text) via getContrastColor()
2. All header wash text contrast ratios >= 12:1 (excellent) because tint opacity is only 18% max
3. All text tokens (text-text, text-muted-foreground, text-subtle) are theme-aware and switch properly
4. NodeBadges uses dark: Tailwind variants which needed proper wiring to the .dark class

#### Bug found and resolved:
Tailwind CSS 4 dark mode variant not wired to .dark class.
NodeBadges.tsx uses dark:text-blue-400, dark:text-amber-400, dark:text-emerald-400.
Tailwind CSS 4 defaults dark: to @media (prefers-color-scheme: dark), not class-based.
The app uses .dark class on html (set by ThemeProvider).
Without @custom-variant dark, badge text colors would follow system preference instead of app theme.
Resolution: Added @custom-variant dark to src/index.css

#### Visual Verification (5 themes tested):
1. Dark theme: Service (blue), Object Storage (lime), Message Queue (orange) - all text readable
2. Light theme: All 7 node types (blue, green, purple, orange, purple/cloud, lime, cyan) - all readable
3. Rose Pine Dawn (light): 3 nodes tested - all text readable
4. Nord (dark): 3 nodes tested - all text readable
5. Catppuccin Mocha (dark): 3 nodes tested - all text readable

#### Text elements verified:
- Display names (text-text)
- Type labels (text-muted-foreground on bg-highlight-med)
- Argument keys (text-muted-foreground)
- Argument values (text-subtle)
- Icon badges (getContrastColor auto-contrast)
- Badge colors (dark: variant now correctly wired)

#### Build: Clean (no CSS or new TypeScript errors)
#### Commit: 8ede9ee
#### Feature #366 marked passing

## Session: Feature #383 - Canvas Performance Optimization for iPad
Date: 2026-03-05

### Feature #383: Canvas Performance Optimization for iPad - PASSING

#### Implementation:

**src/hooks/useCanvasPerformance.ts (NEW):**
- LOD state based on zoom level (LOD_ZOOM_THRESHOLD = 0.4, LOD_EDGE_THRESHOLD = 0.35)
- prefers-reduced-motion media query detection with change listener
- FPS monitoring (requestAnimationFrame-based, toggle-able)
- Node count tracking with warning threshold (NODE_COUNT_WARNING = 100)
- Canvas bounds constant (CANVAS_BOUNDS: [-10000, -10000] to [10000, 10000])

**src/components/nodes/SimplifiedNode.tsx (NEW):**
- Low-detail node: simple colored rectangle with display name
- Minimal handles (in/out only), no port details
- No animations or transitions for maximum performance
- Uses effective color from nodeColors utility

**src/components/nodes/lodNodeTypeMap.ts (NEW):**
- Maps all 16 node types to SimplifiedNode for LOD rendering

**src/contexts/CanvasPerformanceContext.tsx (NEW):**
- React Context providing isLowDetailMode, isLowDetailEdges, prefersReducedMotion
- Used by edge components to avoid prop drilling

**src/components/canvas/FpsCounter.tsx (NEW):**
- Dev-mode overlay: FPS (color-coded), node count, zoom %, LOD status, reduced motion
- Monospace font, dark translucent background with backdrop blur

**src/components/canvas/Canvas.tsx (MODIFIED):**
- Integrated useCanvasPerformance hook
- LOD node type switching: lodNodeTypes when zoom < 0.4, regular nodeTypes otherwise
- translateExtent={CANVAS_BOUNDS} prevents infinite panning
- Node count monitoring effect: shows toast warning at > 100 nodes
- Zoom tracking via onMoveEnd callback
- FpsCounter overlay (when enabled)
- CanvasPerformanceContext.Provider wraps ReactFlow

**src/components/edges/SyncEdge.tsx (MODIFIED):**
- LOD: renders thin line without labels when isLowDetailEdges
- Respects prefersReducedMotion: disables transitions

**src/components/edges/AsyncEdge.tsx (MODIFIED):**
- LOD: renders simple dashed line without animation or labels
- Respects prefersReducedMotion: disables flow animation and transitions

**src/components/edges/DataFlowEdge.tsx (MODIFIED):**
- LOD: renders thinner line without labels
- Respects prefersReducedMotion: disables transitions

#### Feature Steps Verification:
1. ✅ Level-of-detail: at low zoom, SimplifiedNode renders colored rectangles
2. ✅ translateExtent limits canvas bounds (prevents infinite panning)
3. ✅ Node count monitoring: toast warning at > 100 visible nodes
4. ✅ prefers-reduced-motion: animations and transitions disabled when enabled
5. ✅ Edge simplification: straight thin lines at low zoom levels
6. ✅ FPS counter in dev mode (toggle-able overlay)

#### Build: Clean (npx vite build passes)
#### Console: No errors from performance code (only pre-existing SSL/PWA)

#### Implementation:
- Created `src/analyze/graphBuilder.ts`:
  - `buildGraph(inferenceResult, textApi, registry, options)` main function
  - `resolveNodeType()` maps AI-inferred types to registry types with fallback synonyms
  - Comprehensive TYPE_FALLBACK_MAP covering ~90 common synonyms (microservice→service, lambda→function, postgres→database, kafka→event-bus, etc.)
  - Creates nodes via textApi.addNode() with resolved types and displayNames
  - Creates child nodes recursively for hierarchical structures
  - Creates edges via textApi.addEdge() mapping SYNC→sync, ASYNC→async, DATA_FLOW→data-flow
  - Attaches code references via textApi.addCodeRef() mapping SOURCE→source, API_SPEC→api-spec, etc.
  - Adds AI-generated description notes to nodes via textApi.addNote()
  - Applies auto-layout using computeElkLayout from elkLayout.ts
  - Returns BuildResult with nodesCreated, edgesCreated, codeRefsAttached, warnings[], nodeIdMap
- Created `test/unit/analyze/graphBuilder.test.ts` with 31 tests covering:
  - resolveNodeType: exact types, short names, synonyms, unknown types, case-insensitivity

  - Notes: description notes, disabling notes, custom author
  - Hierarchy: child node creation
  - Edge warnings: missing source/target nodes
  - Architecture metadata: name and description
  - Auto-layout: applied by default, skippable
  - Fallback type mapping: unknown types, synonym types
  - Return value: correct counts, empty results

## Session: Feature #349 - Analysis Prompt Template System
Date: 2026-03-05

### Feature #349: Analysis Prompt Template System - PASSING

#### Implementation:
- Created `src/analyze/prompts/` directory with 7 files:
  - `types.ts`: PromptTemplate interface with systemPrompt, analysisSteps[], responseSchema, postProcessing, fewShotExamples
  - `shared.ts`: NODE_TYPE_REGISTRY_TEXT (all built-in node types), STANDARD_RESPONSE_SCHEMA, 3 few-shot examples (web app, microservices, data pipeline)
  - `general.ts`: Language-agnostic default template, fallback for any project type
  - `webApp.ts`: Specialized for frontend/backend web apps (React, Next.js, Django, Rails, etc.)
  - `microservices.ts`: Specialized for distributed systems with Docker/K8s, service boundaries, event-driven patterns
  - `dataPipeline.ts`: Specialized for ETL, data processing, analytics (Airflow, Spark, dbt)
  - `index.ts`: Template registry with auto-selection (matcher scoring), manual override, custom template registration, config file loading

#### Key design decisions:
- Templates use {{placeholder}} tokens ({{projectProfile}}, {{fileContents}}) for runtime substitution
- Auto-selection uses scorer functions returning 0-100, highest score wins (minimum threshold 20 to beat general)
- Custom templates via registerCustomTemplate() with optional matcher, or loadCustomTemplatesFromConfig() for .archcanvas.yml
- All templates include NODE_TYPE_REGISTRY_TEXT with full namespace/name listing of all built-in types
- Few-shot examples are valid JSON that can be parsed and validated against inferenceResultSchema

## Session: Feature #348 - Incremental Re-analysis and Merge
Date: 2026-03-05

### Feature #348: Incremental Re-analysis and Merge - PASSING

#### Implementation:
- Created `src/analyze/merge.ts` with core merge logic:
  - `matchNodes()`: Two-pass node matching (code-ref paths, then display names)
  - `mergeAnalysis()`: Non-destructive merge producing MergeResult
  - `applyMerge()`: Applies MergeResult to produce new ArchGraph
  - Node matching by overlapping code-ref paths (pass 1) and normalized display names (pass 2)
  - Edge matching translating inferred node IDs to existing node IDs
  - Three conflict resolution strategies: ai-wins, manual-wins, prompt
  - Preserves manually created nodes/edges (never flagged as removed)
  - AI-inferred unmatched nodes flagged as "possibly removed" with pending notes
  - New inferred nodes added with "newly-detected" notes
  - Code ref updates tracked for matched nodes
  - Type change detection with strategy-dependent handling
- CLI `--merge` and `--strategy` flags already wired by prior agent (feature #346)
- MCP `merge` and `strategy` options already wired by prior agent (feature #347)
- Created `test/unit/analyze/merge.test.ts` with 30 tests:
  - matchNodes: code-ref matching, display-name matching, unmatched existing/inferred, preference for code-ref, type change detection
  - mergeAnalysis: simple merge summary, manual node preservation, AI node flagging, code ref updates, type changes with both strategies, edge addition/preservation/flagging, manual edge preservation
  - applyMerge: new node addition, code ref updates, type update with ai-wins, type preservation with manual-wins, possibly-removed notes, edge addition, edge flagging, immutability, newly-detected notes, renamed components, removed components, new components, skip notes option

#### Verification:
- Vitest: 30/30 tests passing
- All 296 analyze tests pass (no regressions)

## Session: Feature #435 - Consolidate Duplicate Logic and Improve Reuse
Date: 2026-03-05

### Feature #435: Consolidate Duplicate Logic and Improve Reuse - PASSING

#### Duplications Identified and Consolidated:

1. **Inline Edit Logic (7 node components -> 1 hook)**
   - All 7 node components (GenericNode, HexagonNode, CloudNode, CylinderNode, DocumentNode, ParallelogramNode, StadiumNode) had identical inline editing state management (~30 lines each)
   - Extracted to `src/hooks/useInlineEdit.ts` custom hook
   - Provides: isInlineEditing, editValue, setEditValue, inputRef, confirmEdit, revertEdit, handleKeyDown

2. **Icon Map (embedded in GenericNode -> dedicated module)**
   - `iconMap` was defined in GenericNode.tsx but imported by 6 shape nodes + CommandPalette + QuickSearch
   - Extracted to `src/components/nodes/iconMap.ts`
   - GenericNode re-exports for backward compatibility

3. **Port Handle Rendering (7 components -> 2 shared components)**
   - All shaped nodes had identical port handle rendering logic (~60 lines each)
   - Created `src/components/nodes/NodePortHandles.tsx` with:
     - `ShapedPortHandles`: For shape-aware positioning (hexagon, cloud, etc.)
     - `GenericPortHandles`: For percentage-based positioning (GenericNode)

4. **Node Inner Content (6 shaped nodes -> 1 shared component)**
   - All shaped nodes had identical inner content (header, ref indicator, args, badges)
   - Created `src/components/nodes/NodeContent.tsx`
   - Customizable via className props for shape-specific padding/alignment

5. **Edge Components (3 near-identical components -> 1 factory)**
   - AsyncEdge, SyncEdge, DataFlowEdge shared identical structure
   - Created `src/components/edges/createEdgeComponent.tsx` factory
   - Each edge now just provides a config object (color, width, dash, animation)

6. **Barrel Files Added:**
   - `src/components/nodes/index.ts` (all node exports)
   - `src/components/edges/index.ts` (all edge exports)
   - `src/hooks/index.ts` (all hook exports)

#### Impact:
- 850 insertions, 1654 deletions = **net reduction of 804 lines**
- 6 shaped nodes reduced from ~270 lines each to ~78 lines each
- 3 edge components reduced from ~50 lines each to ~17 lines each
- No circular dependencies introduced (verified with madge)

## Session: Feature #440 - Review and Clean Up Zustand Store Architecture
Date: 2026-03-05

### Feature #440: Review and Clean Up Zustand Store Architecture - PASSING

#### Store Architecture Audit Results:

**7 Zustand stores mapped:**
1. **coreStore** (~1350 lines) - Graph state, mutations, file ops, undo/redo, engine instances
2. **canvasStore** (~207 lines) - Selection, viewport, zoom, layout spacing
3. **uiStore** (~572 lines) - Panels, dialogs, modals, placement mode, connect mode, toasts, theme
4. **aiStore** (~139 lines) - AI conversations, messages
5. **navigationStore** (~28 lines) - Fractal zoom navigation path
6. **annotationStore** (~137 lines) - Drawing mode, strokes, undo stack
7. **pencilStore** (~78 lines) - Apple Pencil pressure/tilt state

**Cross-store dependencies:** coreStore → canvasStore, uiStore, aiStore (for save/open operations)

**Slice boundaries: LOGICAL** - Each store has a clear domain. No state duplication across stores except `selectedNodeId`/`selectedNodeIds` backward-compat pattern in canvasStore (intentional and documented).

**Broad subscriptions: NONE** - All 54 consuming files use granular selectors `(s) => s.field`.

#### Changes Made:

1. **Created `src/store/selectors.ts`** - 40+ centralized, documented selectors:
   - Direct selectors: selectGraph, selectIsDirty, selectFileName, selectNodeCount, etc.
   - Derived selectors: selectHasSelection, selectHasNodeSelection, selectIsConnectMode, selectHasOpenDialog, selectIsAtRoot, selectNavigationDepth
   - Barrel exported via `src/store/index.ts`

2. **Fixed hardcoded `rightPanelWidth: 320` in `_getCanvasStateForSave`** - Now reads actual value from uiStore

3. **Removed duplicate panel constants from `utils/constants.ts`** - LEFT_PANEL_DEFAULT_WIDTH, LEFT_PANEL_MIN_WIDTH, RIGHT_PANEL_DEFAULT_WIDTH, RIGHT_PANEL_MIN_WIDTH were duplicated (originals live in uiStore, constants.ts copies never imported)

4. **Updated legacy comments** - Clarified purpose of static default width constants

5. **Added 47 tests** in `test/unit/store/storeSelectors.test.ts`:
   - Core, Canvas, UI, AI, Navigation, Annotation selector tests
   - Store architecture boundary verification tests
   - Selector stability verification
   - nodeCount/edgeCount mutation tracking test

Date: 2026-03-08
Status: PASSING

### Feature #450: Cross-File Navigation Stack - PASSING

#### Implementation (verified existing from prior commit):

1. **nestedCanvasStore** (`src/store/nestedCanvasStore.ts`):
   - `FileStackEntry` interface: filePath, graph, navigationPath, viewport
   - `fileStack: FileStackEntry[]` - stack of saved file states
   - `activeFilePath: string | null` - currently active file
   - `pushFile(filePath, graph)` - saves current state, switches to new graph
   - `popFile()` - restores previous file's graph, navigation path, viewport
   - `popToRoot()` - returns directly to root from any depth
   - `getDepth()` - returns fileStack.length (0 = root)
   - `getStackEntry(index)` - access specific stack level
   - `reset()` - clear all navigation state

2. **Store integration**:
   - Uses coreStore._setGraph() to swap active graph on push/pop
   - Uses navigationStore.zoomToRoot()/zoomToLevel() for path management
   - Uses canvasStore.setViewport()/requestFitView() for viewport restoration
   - Barrel export updated in src/store/index.ts

     getStackEntry, popToRoot, reset, combined file+nav paths, viewport restoration
   - All tests passing

### Feature #451: Zoom-Into-Bounds Animation - PASSING

#### Implementation (verified existing):

1. **useContainerDiveIn hook** (`src/hooks/useContainerDiveIn.ts`):
   - `calculateNodeFillViewport()`: Computes viewport to center+zoom node with padding
   - `diveIn()`: Multi-phase animation: zoom-in (350ms) → crossfade-in (150ms) → file switch → crossfade-out (150ms)
   - `diveOut()`: Reverse animation: zoom-out-fade → pop file → zoom-out → idle

   - TransitionOverlay component rendered with phase/color from diveState

   - Phases: idle, zoom-in, crossfade-in, crossfade-out, zoom-out-fade, zoom-out
   - CSS opacity transitions with configurable duration (default 150ms)
   - Radial gradient + backdrop blur visual effect
   - Callbacks for phase completion (onCrossfadeInComplete, onCrossfadeOutComplete)

## Session: Feature #476 - Built-in AI initialization flow (API key path)
Date: 2026-03-08
Status: PASSING

### Summary:
Created `src/ai/initWithAI.ts` — the orchestration module that wires the agentic loop
engine with codebase analysis to provide in-app AI-powered project initialization.

### What was built:

1. **initWithAI() function** (`src/ai/initWithAI.ts`):
   - Full orchestration: scan → detect → select → prompt → agentic loop → result
   - Phase 1 (Scanning): Uses scanDirectoryBrowser to traverse project files via File System Access API
   - Phase 2 (Detecting): Uses detectProject to identify project type, languages, frameworks
   - Phase 3 (Selecting): Uses selectKeyFilesBrowser to choose architecturally significant files
   - Phase 4 (Prompting + Building): Builds system/user prompts via initArchitecture.ts,
     wires MCP tool handlers to TextApi, runs runAgentLoop so Claude iteratively builds the graph
   - Emits InitWithAIProgress events throughout all phases for UI consumption
   - Returns InitWithAIResult with graph, stats, projectProfile, toolCalls, warnings

2. **Tool registry construction** (buildToolRegistry):
   - Filters TOOL_DEFINITIONS to INIT_TOOL_NAMES (16 tools for architecture init)
   - Excludes save, file_info, analyze_codebase (not relevant in-browser)
   - Wires each tool handler to dispatchToolCall with ToolHandlerContext

3. **Progress tracking**:
   - Tracks nodesCreated, edgesCreated, codeRefsLinked from tool calls
   - Emits building progress with tool call details
   - Forwards onToolCall callback to caller

4. **Error handling**:
   - Scan/detect/select errors wrapped with phase context
   - Tool call errors collected as warnings
   - Max iteration guard adds warning about incomplete graph
   - AbortSignal checked at each phase boundary and passed to agentic loop

### Tests: 21 tests (all passing)
- test/unit/ai/initWithAI.test.ts
- Orchestration: full flow, project metadata, registry, agent loop options
- Progress: phase order, monotonic percentages, building events per tool call
- Tool calls: onToolCall callback, tool call log, error warnings
- Max iterations: warning message
- Abort: signal propagation, immediate abort
- Errors: scan failure, detection failure, file selection failure
- Tool registry: excludes save/file_info/analyze_codebase, wires to dispatchToolCall
- Directory listing: builds tree from scan result
- Defaults: folder name as architecture name, code ref counting

## Feature #489: Fix mcpJsonBrowser imports node:path via mcpJson.ts - PASSING

### Summary:
Fixed a bug where the browser MCP auto-registration silently failed because
mcpJsonBrowser.ts imported from mcpJson.ts which has a top-level
`import { dirname } from 'node:path'`. Vite externalizes node:path for browser
builds, causing the import to throw.

### Root Cause:
Shared constants (ARCHCANVAS_SERVER_KEY) and types (McpServerEntry, McpJsonFile)
were co-located with Node.js-only code in mcpJson.ts.

### Fix:
1. Created `src/mcp/mcpJsonShared.ts` — browser-safe module with shared constants/types
2. Updated `src/mcp/mcpJson.ts` — imports from mcpJsonShared, re-exports for backward compat
3. Updated `src/mcp/mcpJsonBrowser.ts` — imports from mcpJsonShared instead of mcpJson
4. Updated `src/store/projectStore.ts` — added .catch() to dynamic import for error logging

### Verification:
- 34/34 MCP JSON tests pass (mcpJson + mcpJsonBrowser)
- 356/356 CLI tests pass (no regressions)
- TypeScript: 0 new errors in source files
- Browser: App loads, zero app console errors (only pre-existing SSL/PWA warnings)
- No mock data patterns in production code

## Feature #491: Fix CLI entry point _isDirectRun symlink detection - PASSING

### Summary:
The _isDirectRun guard in src/cli/index.ts compared import.meta.url (real file path)
against process.argv[1] (potentially a symlink path). Through npm link, these never
match, so main() never executes and all CLI commands produce zero output.

### Fix:
- Added `import { realpathSync } from 'node:fs'`
- Wrapped detection in IIFE with try/catch
- Uses `realpathSync(process.argv[1])` to resolve symlinks before comparison
- Falls back to old endsWith comparison if realpathSync throws

### Changes:

1. **src/cli/index.ts** - Replaced lines 411-414:
   - Old: `import.meta.url.endsWith(process.argv[1].replace(/\\/g, '/'))`
   - New: `realpathSync(process.argv[1])` → `new URL('file://' + resolved)` → compare

2. **test/unit/cli/cliEntryPoint.test.ts** - Added 5 new tests:
   - Uses realpathSync from node:fs
   - Calls realpathSync on process.argv[1]
   - Converts to file:// URL
   - Has fallback when realpathSync throws
   - Does not run main() when imported by vitest

### Verification:
- 361/361 CLI tests pass (5 new, 356 existing)
- Built CLI: `node dist/cli/index.js --help` produces help output
- Built CLI: `archcanvas mcp --file` responds to JSON-RPC initialize
- Built CLI: `archcanvas init` creates .archc file
- Browser: App loads, zero app console errors (only pre-existing SSL/PWA)

#### Commit: 71e214b
#### Feature #491 marked passing
#### Progress: 491/491 features passing (100%)

## Feature #499: Implement git repo fetcher and .archc resolver - PASSING

### Summary:
Created a new module that fetches a git repository's main.archc file at a specific
tag/commit ref, parses it using the existing protobuf codec, and returns the
architecture data. Supports public repos on GitHub, GitLab, and unknown hosts via
fallback URL patterns.

### New Files:

1. **src/core/git/repoFetcher.ts** — Git repo fetcher module:
   - `parseRepoUrl()` — parses HTTPS/SSH git URLs into platform/owner/repo
   - `fetchRepoArchc()` — main API: fetches and decodes main.archc from remote repo
   - GitHub strategy: Uses GitHub Contents API with raw binary response
   - GitLab strategy: Uses GitLab Repository Files API
   - Unknown host fallback: Tries common raw URL patterns (Gitea, cgit)
   - Error hierarchy: RepoFetchError > RepoNotFoundError, RefNotFoundError,
     ArchcNotFoundError, RepoNotPublicError
   - Dependency-injectable fetch function for testability
   - Configurable timeout (default 30s)

2. **test/unit/core/repoFetcher.test.ts** — 34 tests:
   - URL parsing: GitHub/GitLab HTTPS, SSH, .git suffix, trailing slash, unknown hosts
   - Validation: empty/whitespace URL and ref
   - GitHub success: fetch + parse, ref query param
   - GitHub errors: repo not found, ref not found, archc not found, 403, 500
   - GitLab: correct API endpoint, repo not found, 403
   - Unknown host fallback: raw URL patterns, all-fail error
   - .archc parsing: invalid binary, multi-node graphs, raw data return
   - Error types: inheritance, names, stored properties

### Feature steps covered:
1. ✅ Repo fetcher module accepting URL + ref
2. ✅ GitHub API fetching (Contents API)
3. ✅ Fallback via raw URL patterns for non-GitHub repos
4. ✅ Validates main.archc exists at repo root
5. ✅ Parses fetched .archc using existing protobuf deserialization
6. ✅ Returns parsed architecture data for caching
7. ✅ Handles all error cases: repo/ref/file not found, not public

### Verification:
- 34/34 new tests pass
- 1036/1036 core tests pass (0 regressions)
- Browser: App loads with 42 nodedefs, zero app console errors (only pre-existing SSL/PWA)
- No mock data patterns in production code
